  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:12pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Schedules Fourth-Quarter Financial Results Conference Call for February 7</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">San Antonio, Texas, January 10, 2025 &#x2015;</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> Victory Capital Holdings, Inc. (NASDAQ: VCTR) (&#x201c;Victory Capital&#x201d; or the &#x201c;Company&#x201d;) today reported Total Assets Under Management (AUM) of $171.9 billion, Other Assets of $4.2 billion, and Total Client Assets of $176.1 billion, as of December 31, 2024.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:justify;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">For the month of December, average Total AUM was $175.8 billion, average Other Assets was $4.2 billion, and average Total Client Assets was $174.5 billion.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:justify;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">For the fourth quarter, the Company reported long-term AUM net flows of -$1.7 billion.</font></p>

  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;vertical-align:super;font-size:6.03pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">2</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Total AUM includes both discretionary assets under management and non-discretionary assets under advisement and excludes Other Assets.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;vertical-align:super;font-size:6.03pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">3</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Includes institutional and retail share classes, money market and VIP funds.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;vertical-align:super;font-size:6.03pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">4</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Includes wrap program accounts, CITs, UMAs, UCITS, private funds, and non-U.S. domiciled pooled vehicles.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;vertical-align:super;font-size:6.03pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">5</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Represents only ETF assets held by third parties and excludes ETF assets held by other Victory Capital products.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;vertical-align:super;font-size:6.03pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">6</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:9pt;font-family:Arial;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Includes low-fee (2 to 4 bps) institutional assets, previously reported in the Solutions asset class within the by asset class table and in Separate Accounts and Other Pooled Vehicles within the by vehicle table.   <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Fourth-Quarter Conference Call and Webcast Details</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Victory Capital will report fourth-quarter 2024 financial results after the market closes on Thursday, February 6, 2025. Victory Capital&#x2019;s earnings release and supplemental materials will be available on the investor relations section of the Company&#x2019;s website at </font><font style="color:#0000ff;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">https://ir.vcm.com </font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">before the conference call begins.</font><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">To participate in the conference call, please call 1-800-715-9871 (domestic) or 1-646-307-1963 (international), shortly before 8:00 a.m. ET and reference the Victory Capital Conference Call.   <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">About Victory Capital</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Victory Capital is a diversified global asset management firm with total assets under management of $171.9 billion, and $176.1 billion in total client assets, as of December 31, 2024. The Company employs a next-generation business strategy that combines boutique investment qualities with the benefits of a fully integrated, centralized operating and distribution platform.</font></p>
  <p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:6pt;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:6pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="color:#000000;white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11pt;font-family:Arial;min-width:fit-content;">Victory Capital provides specialized investment strategies to institutions, intermediaries, retirement platforms and individual investors. With 11 autonomous Investment Franchises and a Solutions Business, Victory Capital offers a wide array of investment products and services, including mutual funds, ETFs, separately managed accounts, alternative investments, third-party ETF model strategies, collective investment trusts, private funds, a 529 Education Savings Plan, and brokerage services.</font></p>
